## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (rate laws / mass-action ODE models)
**Analysis**: The target dA_dt is the time-derivative of a concentration A, indicating an ordinary differential equation rate law for reaction kinetics. With only t and A available, plausible models are single-species decay/production laws, possibly with explicit time-dependent rate coefficients or relaxation to equilibrium.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order consumption: dA_dt = -c0 (surface-limited or saturated reagent; A decreases linearly in time)
- First-order decay (unimolecular): dA_dt = -c0 * A (radioactive-like decay; exponential A(t))
- Second-order decay (bimolecular with equal reactants): dA_dt = -c0 * A**2 (A(t) follows 1/(t) behavior)
- n-th order power-law rate: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 (empirical/fractional order kinetics)
- Mixed order (parallel pathways): dA_dt = -c0 * A - c1 * A**2 (simultaneous unimolecular + bimolecular loss)
- Relaxation to equilibrium (linear reversible net rate): dA_dt = c0 * (c1 - A) (approach to steady-state concentration c1)
- Autocatalytic / Prout–Tompkins-type: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (self-accelerating then self-limiting kinetics)
- Time-dependent first-order rate (linear ramp): dA_dt = -(c0 + c1 * t) * A (changing conditions or catalyst activation/deactivation over time)
- Time-dependent first-order rate (exponential modulation): dA_dt = -c0 * exp(c1 * t) * A (accelerating or decelerating effective rate constant)
- Damped oscillatory forcing on rate: dA_dt = -c0 * A + c1 * sin(c2 * t) (periodic driving/perturbation affecting net production)
- Autoinhibition / self-poisoning polynomial: dA_dt = -c0 * A - c1 * A**3 (stronger-than-second-order inhibition at high A)
- General polynomial-in-A kinetics: dA_dt = c0 + c1 * A + c2 * A**2 + c3 * A**3 (local approximation to complex mechanisms)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- If A(t) is exponential (straight line in log(A) vs t), prefer dA_dt proportional to A (first-order form -c*A).
- If 1/A vs t is roughly linear, prefer a dominant second-order term dA_dt proportional to -A**2.
- If A decreases nearly linearly with t over a wide range, include a constant term (zero-order: dA_dt ≈ -c0).
- If the decay rate slows dramatically at low A (tailing), consider orders c1 < 1 in -c0*A**c1 (fractional order / diffusion limitation proxy).
- A nonzero steady state A→c1 suggests a restoring form c0*(c1 - A) (net reversible/chemostatted behavior).
- Sigmoidal time-courses (slow start then acceleration then slowdown) are consistent with autocatalytic terms like c0*A*(c1 - A).
- Curvature changes in log(A) vs t often indicate parallel pathways (e.g., -c0*A - c1*A**2) rather than a single order.
- If apparent rate changes systematically over time at fixed A-range, include explicit t-dependence in the rate coefficient, e.g., (c0 + c1*t) or exp(c1*t) multiplying A.
- Small periodic ripples around a trend in A(t) can be captured by additive sinusoidal forcing in dA_dt (experimental cycling/perturbations).

Final search results
============================================================
Best expression     : A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1)
Structure desc      : Purely multiplicative in A with a time-varying coefficient via log(1+c2 t): A*(c0 + c1 log(1+c2 t)). A appears only linearly as a global factor; t appears only inside the logarithm. With c2≈0.942 and moderate c1≈0.0623, the behavior is essentially a linear-in-A scaling whose slope increases slowly with t; no term degenerates (and the fit suggests this is effectively exact).
Fitted params       : c0=-1.3626e-01, c1=6.2258e-02, c2=9.4234e-01
Train NMSE          : 2.13e-15
Test NMSE           : 2.02e-15
OOD Test NMSE       : 2.91e-14

============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (CRK35)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A + c1*_q*A*log(c2*t + c3)
Candidate formulas: 53

GT is the fixed function
\[
f(t,A)=A\Big(\alpha\log(\beta t+1)-\gamma\Big)
\]
with \(\alpha=0.062258070344434831\), \(\beta=0.9423435234237035\), \(\gamma=0.13625696690019862\).
So GT is **linear in \(A\)**, has **no \(A\)-independent terms**, and its only \(t\)-dependence is \(\log(\beta t+1)\).

Below, a candidate matches iff we can choose its constants so the expression becomes exactly \(A(\alpha\log(\beta t+1)-\gamma)\) for all \(t,A\). Any extra term depending on \(t\) or \(A\) must be eliminable by setting its coefficient to 0 (or otherwise making it identically 0).

---

### 1. \(A*c0 + A*c1*\log(c2*t + 1)\)
This is exactly \(A(c0 + c1\log(c2 t+1))\).  
Choose \(c1=\alpha\), \(c2=\beta\), \(c0=-\gamma\). Matches.

### 2. \(A*c0 + A*c1*\log(c2*t + 1) + A*c3\)
Combine \(A*c0 + A*c3 = A(c0+c3)\).  
Choose \(c1=\alpha\), \(c2=\beta\), and \(c0+c3=-\gamma\) (many solutions). Matches.

### 3. \(A*c0 + A*c1*t + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + A*c4*exp(c5*sin(c6*log(c7*t + 1) + c8))\)
To match GT, must remove \(t\), \(\exp\), and oscillatory terms: set \(c1=0, c2=0, c4=0\). Then becomes \(A*c0\), which cannot produce the required \(A\log(\beta t+1)\) term. No match.

### 4. \(A*c0 + A*c1*t + A**c2*c3*log(c4*t + 1)\)
Need no linear-in-\(t\) term: set \(c1=0\).  
Need linear in \(A\): set \(c2=1\), then term is \(A*c3\log(c4 t+1)\).  
Choose \(c3=\alpha\), \(c4=\beta\), \(c0=-\gamma\). Matches.

### 5. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + A*c3 + A*c4*t\)
Must remove \(A*t\): set \(c4=0\). Then reduce to case like (2). Matches (pick \(c1=\alpha,c2=\beta,c0+c3=-\gamma\)).

### 6. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + c3*log(c4*(c5*t + 1)**c6 + 1)\)
GT has **no \(A\)-independent term**. The last term is \(A\)-independent and depends on \(t\) unless eliminated. Set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 7. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + c3\)
Constant \(c3\) is \(A\)-independent; GT has none, so must set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 8. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + A*c3 + c4\)
Must set \(c4=0\) (no \(A\)-independent constant). Then reduces to (2). Matches.

### 9. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + c3 + c4*(c5*t + 1)**c6\)
The last two terms are \(A\)-independent; GT has none. Set \(c3=0\) and \(c4=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 10. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + A*c3/(A + c4)\)
The extra term \(A*c3/(A+c4)\) is not linear in \(A\) unless it is identically 0. Set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 11. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + c3*sin(c4*t + c5)\)
Sine term is \(A\)-independent; must set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 12. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + A*c3 + A*c4*t + c5\)
Need remove \(A*t\): set \(c4=0\). Need remove constant: set \(c5=0\). Then reduces to (2). Matches.

### 13. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + A*c3/(A + c4) + c5\)
Set \(c3=0\) to remove nonlinearity in \(A\). Set \(c5=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 14. \(A*c0 + A**c1*c2*log(c3*t + 1) + c4 + c5*log(c6*t + 1)*cos(c7*t)\)
Must remove \(A\)-independent terms: set \(c4=0\) and \(c5=0\).  
Need linear in \(A\): set \(c1=1\), then \(A*c2\log(c3 t+1)\).  
Choose \(c2=\alpha\), \(c3=\beta\), \(c0=-\gamma\). Matches.

### 15. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + c3*exp(c4*t)*log(c5*t + 1)\)
Last term is \(A\)-independent; must set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 16. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + A**c3*c4/(A**c3 + c5) + c6\)
Need remove \(A\)-dependent rational term: set \(c4=0\). Need remove constant: set \(c6=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 17. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + c3*exp(c4*sin(c5*t + c6))\)
Extra term is \(A\)-independent; set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 18. \(A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2*log(c3*t + 1)\)
GT has no \(A^2\) term: set \(c0=0\). Then expression is \(A(c1 + c2\log(c3 t+1))\).  
Choose \(c2=\alpha\), \(c3=\beta\), \(c1=-\gamma\). Matches.

### 19. \(A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2*log(c3*t + 1) + A*c4\)
Set \(c0=0\). Combine \(A*c1 + A*c4 = A(c1+c4)\). Choose \(c2=\alpha\), \(c3=\beta\), \(c1+c4=-\gamma\). Matches.

### 20. \(A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2*log(c3*t + 1) + A*c4 + c5\)
Set \(c0=0\). Must remove constant: set \(c5=0\). Then as (19). Matches.

### 21. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + c3 + c4*sin(c5*t + c6)\)
Must remove \(A\)-independent terms: set \(c3=0\), \(c4=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 22. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + c3 + c4*log(c5*t + c6*exp(c7*t) + 1)\)
Extra \(A\)-independent terms: set \(c3=0\), \(c4=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 23. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + c3 + c4*exp(c5*sin(c6*log(c7*t + 1) + c8))\)
Set \(c3=0\), \(c4=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 24. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + c3*sin(A*c4 + c5*log(c6*t + 1) + c7)\)
Sine term depends on \(A\) and \(t\) in a non-GT way; only safe elimination is \(c3=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 25. \(A*c0 + A*c1*t + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + A*c4*log(c5*t + 1)*cos(c6*t)\)
To match GT, must eliminate \(t\), \(\exp\), and cosine-modulated term: set \(c1=0,c2=0,c4=0\). Leaves \(A*c0\) only, cannot create \(A\log(\beta t+1)\). No match.

### 26. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5\)
Need remove constant: \(c5=0\). Need remove \(A\exp(c4 t)\): set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 27. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + A*c3*exp(c4*t)\)
Set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 28. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + c3*exp(c4*t)*cos(c5*log(c6*t + 1) + c7)\)
Extra term is \(A\)-independent; set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 29. \(A*c0 + A*c1*sin(c2*log(c3*t + 1) + c4) + c5*exp(c6*t)\)
No log term of the right form; sine and exp terms cannot become \(\log(\beta t+1)\) for all \(t\) by parameter choice. If set \(c1=0,c5=0\), left with \(A*c0\) only. No match.

### 30. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + c3 + c4*exp(c5*t)*log(A*c6 + 1)\)
GT has no \(A\)-independent constant: set \(c3=0\). The last term depends on \(A\) via \(\log(Ac6+1)\) and on \(t\) via \(\exp(c5 t)\); cannot equal 0 for all \(A,t\) unless \(c4=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 31. \(A*c0 + A*c1/(A + c2) + A**c3*c4*log(c5*t + 1) + c6*exp(c7*t)\)
Need remove \(A\)-independent exp term: set \(c6=0\). Need remove \(A*c1/(A+c2)\): set \(c1=0\).  
Need linear in \(A\): set \(c3=1\), giving \(A*c4\log(c5 t+1)\).  
Choose \(c4=\alpha\), \(c5=\beta\), \(c0=-\gamma\). Matches.

### 32. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + A**c3*c4*exp(c5*t) + c6\)
Set \(c6=0\). Extra \(A^{c3}\exp(c5 t)\) must vanish: set \(c4=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 33. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + c3 + c4*sin(A*c5 + c6)*cos(c7*t)\)
Set \(c3=0\). The oscillatory term must vanish: set \(c4=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 34. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + c3 + c4*sin(c5*log(c6*Abs(A) + 1) + c7)\)
Set \(c3=0\). The sine term depends on \(A\) via \(\log(|A|)\); must set \(c4=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 35. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + A**c3*c4\)
Extra \(A^{c3}\) term must be removed: set \(c4=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 36. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + A**c3*c4 + c5\)
Set \(c5=0\) and \(c4=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 37. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + A**c3*c4*log(c5*t + 1)\)
Extra term must vanish: set \(c4=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 38. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + A**c3*c4*log(c5*t + 1) + c6\)
Set \(c6=0\), \(c4=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 39. \(A**2*c0*exp(c1*t)*cos(c2*t) + A*c3 + A**c4*c5*log(c6*t + 1) + c7\)
Need remove constant: \(c7=0\). Need remove \(A^2\) term: set \(c0=0\).  
Need linear in \(A\): set \(c4=1\), giving \(A*c5\log(c6 t+1)\). Then expression is \(A(c3 + c5\log(c6 t+1))\).  
Choose \(c5=\alpha\), \(c6=\beta\), \(c3=-\gamma\). Matches.

### 40. \(A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A**c2*c3 + A**c4*c5*log(c6*t + 1) + c7\)
Need remove constant: \(c7=0\).  
Term \(A*c0*exp(c1 t)\) must not introduce \(\exp\): either set \(c0=0\) (best) or \(c1=0\) making it \(A*c0\).  
Also need only linear \(A\log\) plus linear \(A\) constant: set \(c4=1\) so log term is \(A*c5\log(c6 t+1)\). Set \(c2\) term to supply linear constant or remove: easiest set \(c3=0\) and use \(A*c0\) with \(c1=0\).  
One valid choice: set \(c1=0\) so first term \(A*c0\); set \(c3=0\); set \(c4=1\). Then choose \(c5=\alpha\), \(c6=\beta\), \(c0=-\gamma\). Matches.

### 41. \(A**c0*c1 + A**c2*c3 + A**c4*c5*log(c6*t + 1) + c7\)
Need remove constant: \(c7=0\). Need only one linear-in-\(A\) constant term and one \(A\log\) term.  
Set \(c4=1\) to get \(A*c5\log(c6 t+1)\) with \(c5=\alpha,c6=\beta\).  
For the constant-in-\(t\) linear-in-\(A\) part, set \(c0=1\) so first term \(A*c1\) and choose \(c1=-\gamma\). Eliminate the second power term by setting \(c3=0\). Matches.

### 42. \(A*c0 + A*c1*t + A**c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + A**c5*c6*log(c7*t + 1)\)
Must remove \(A*t\): set \(c1=0\). Must remove exp term: set \(c3=0\).  
Need linear in \(A\) for log term: set \(c5=1\). Then \(A*c6\log(c7 t+1)\).  
Choose \(c6=\alpha\), \(c7=\beta\), \(c0=-\gamma\). Matches.

### 43. \(A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + c3 + c4*exp(c5*t)*sin(c6*t + c7)\)
Set \(c3=0\). Oscillatory exp term must vanish: set \(c4=0\). Then reduces to (1). Matches.

### 44. \(A**c0*c1 + A**c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + A**c5*c6*log(c7*t + 1)\)
Need no exp term: set \(c3=0\).  
Need linear in \(A\) constant term: set \(c0=1\) so first term \(A*c1\) with \(c1=-\gamma\).  
Need linear in \(A\) log term: set \(c5=1\), choose \(c6=\alpha\), \(c7=\beta\). Matches.
